<template>
  <div class="flow-list-container">
    <!-- 搜索区域 -->
    <a-card :bordered="false" class="search-card">
      <a-form layout="vertical">
        <a-row :gutter="8">
          <a-col :xs="24" :sm="24" :md="18" :lg="18" :xl="18">
            <a-form-item :label="!isMobile ? '搜索' : null">
              <a-input
                v-model:value="searchKey"
                :placeholder="isMobile ? '搜索流程名称/编号' : '请输入流程名称/编号搜索'"
                allow-clear
                @pressEnter="handleSearch"
              >
                <template #prefix><SearchOutlined /></template>
              </a-input>
            </a-form-item>
          </a-col>
          <a-col :xs="24" :sm="24" :md="6" :lg="6" :xl="6">
            <div class="btns" :class="{ 'mobile-btns': isMobile }">
              <a-space>
                <a-button type="primary" @click="handleSearch">
                  <template #icon><SearchOutlined /></template>
                  查询
                </a-button>
                <a-button @click="resetSearch">
                  <template #icon><RedoOutlined /></template>
                  重置
                </a-button>
              </a-space>
            </div>
          </a-col>
        </a-row>
      </a-form>
    </a-card>

    <!-- 表格区域 -->
    <a-card :bordered="false" class="table-card">
      <!-- PC端表格 -->
      <a-table
        v-if="!isMobile"
        :columns="columns"
        :data-source="dataList"
        :loading="loading"
        :pagination="pagination"
        @change="handleTableChange"
        rowKey="taskId"
        :scroll="{ x: 'max-content' }"
      >
        <template #bodyCell="{ column, record }">
          <template v-if="column.key === 'businessInfo'">
            <div class="business-info">
              <div class="business-name">{{ record.businessName }}</div>
              <div class="flow-name">{{ record.flowName }}</div>
            </div>
          </template>
          <template v-else-if="column.key === 'nodeInfo'">
            <div>
              <div>{{ record.nodeName }}</div>
              <div class="node-type">{{ getNodeTypeName(record.nodeType) }}</div>
            </div>
          </template>
          <template v-else-if="column.key === 'beginTime'">
            {{ formatDateTime(record.beginTime) }}
          </template>
          <template v-else-if="column.key === 'createTime'">
            {{ formatDateTime(record.createTime) }}
          </template>
          <template v-else-if="column.key === 'action'">
            <a-button type="link" @click="handleProcess(record)">处理</a-button>
          </template>
        </template>
      </a-table>

      <!-- 移动端卡片列表 -->
      <div v-else class="mobile-list">
        <div
          v-for="record in dataList"
          :key="record.taskId"
          class="mobile-card"
          @click="handleProcess(record)"
        >
          <div class="card-header">
            <div class="business-info">
              <div class="business-name">{{ record.businessName }}</div>
              <div class="flow-name">{{ record.flowName }}</div>
            </div>
            <a-badge status="processing" text="待处理" />
          </div>
          <div class="card-body">
            <div class="info-row">
              <span class="label">当前节点：</span>
              <span class="value">{{ record.nodeName }}</span>
              <span class="node-type">{{ getNodeTypeName(record.nodeType) }}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="info-row">
              <span class="label">发起人：</span>
              <span class="value">{{ record.initiatorName }}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="info-row">
              <span class="label">发起时间：</span>
              <span class="value">{{ formatDateTime(record.beginTime) }}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="info-row">
              <span class="label">任务时间：</span>
              <span class="value">{{ formatDateTime(record.createTime) }}</span>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="card-footer">
            <a-button type="primary" size="small">立即处理</a-button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- 移动端分页 -->
        <div class="mobile-pagination">
          <a-pagination
            v-model:current="pagination.current"
            v-model:pageSize="pagination.pageSize"
            :total="pagination.total"
            :showSizeChanger="false"
            :showQuickJumper="false"
            size="small"
            @change="loadData"
          />
          <div class="total-info">共 {{ pagination.total }} 条</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </a-card>

    <!-- 流程处理弹窗 -->
    <FlowProcess
      v-model:visible="processVisible"
      :task-id="currentTaskId"
      :flowInstance-id="currentFlowInstanceId"
      @success="handleProcessSuccess"
    />
  </div>
</template>

<script setup>
import { ref, reactive, onMounted, onBeforeUnmount, computed } from "vue";
import { message } from "ant-design-vue";
import { SearchOutlined, RedoOutlined } from "@ant-design/icons-vue";
import flowInstanceApi from "@/api/biz/bizFlowInstanceApi";
import FlowProcess from "./components/FlowProcess.vue";
import dayjs from "dayjs";

// 节点类型映射
const nodeTypeMap = {
  1: "审批",
  2: "抄送",
  5: "办理",
};

const getNodeTypeName = (type) => nodeTypeMap[type] || "";

// 移动端检测
const isMobile = ref(window.innerWidth <= 768);
const handleResize = () => {
  isMobile.value = window.innerWidth <= 768;
};

onMounted(() => {
  window.addEventListener("resize", handleResize);
  loadData();
});

onBeforeUnmount(() => {
  window.removeEventListener("resize", handleResize);
});

// 时间格式化
const formatDateTime = (date) => {
  if (!date) return "-";
  return dayjs(date).format("YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss");
};

// 查询参数
const searchKey = ref("");

// 列表数据
const loading = ref(false);
const dataList = ref([]);
const pagination = reactive({
  current: 1,
  pageSize: computed(() => (isMobile.value ? 5 : 10)),
  total: 0,
  showSizeChanger: !isMobile.value,
  showQuickJumper: !isMobile.value,
});

// 表格列
const columns = [
  {
    title: "业务信息",
    key: "businessInfo",
    width: 300,
  },
  {
    title: "当前节点",
    key: "nodeInfo",
    width: 200,
  },
  {
    title: "发起人",
    dataIndex: "initiatorName",
    width: 120,
  },
  {
    title: "发起时间",
    key: "beginTime",
    width: 180,
  },
  {
    title: "任务生成时间",
    key: "createTime",
    width: 180,
  },
  {
    title: "操作",
    key: "action",
    width: 100,
    fixed: "right",
  },
];

// 加载数据
const loadData = async () => {
  loading.value = true;
  try {
    const params = {
      Current: pagination.current,
      Size: pagination.pageSize,
      SearchKey: searchKey.value || undefined,
    };
    const res = await flowInstanceApi.getPendingList(params);
    dataList.value = res.records || [];
    pagination.total = res.total || 0;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("加载待审批列表失败", error);
    message.error("加载待审批列表失败");
  } finally {
    loading.value = false;
  }
};

// 搜索
const handleSearch = () => {
  pagination.current = 1;
  loadData();
};

// 重置
const resetSearch = () => {
  searchKey.value = "";
  handleSearch();
};

// 表格变化
const handleTableChange = (pag) => {
  pagination.current = pag.current;
  pagination.pageSize = pag.pageSize;
  loadData();
};

// 处理
const processVisible = ref(false);
const currentTaskId = ref(null);
const currentFlowInstanceId = ref(null);

const handleProcess = (record) => {
  currentTaskId.value = record.taskId;
  currentFlowInstanceId.value = record.flowInstanceId;
  processVisible.value = true;
};

const handleProcessSuccess = () => {
  loadData();
};
</script>

<style lang="scss" scoped>

  // 移动端样式

</style>


<template>
  <a-modal
    :open="visible"
    :title="`流程处理 - ${flowDetail?.flowInstance?.flowName || ''}`"
    :width="1000"
    @ok="handleOk"
    @cancel="handleCancel"
    :confirmLoading="submitting"
    :maskClosable="false"
    destroyOnClose
  >
    <a-spin :spinning="loading">
      <div class="flow-process-container">
        <!-- 流程信息 -->
        <a-card class="flow-info" size="small">
          <a-row :gutter="16">
            <a-col :span="8">
              <div class="info-item">
                <span class="label">流程编号：</span>
                <span class="value">{{ flowDetail?.flowInstance?.code }}</span>
              </div>
            </a-col>
            <a-col :span="8">
              <div class="info-item">
                <span class="label">当前节点：</span>
                <span class="value">{{ flowDetail?.flowInstance?.currentNodeName }}</span>
              </div>
            </a-col>
            <a-col :span="8">
              <div class="info-item">
                <span class="label">发起人：</span>
                <span class="value">{{ flowDetail?.flowInstance?.initiatorName }}</span>
              </div>
            </a-col>
          </a-row>
        </a-card>

        <!-- 使用 DeviceChangeCompare 组件展示变更内容 -->
        <DeviceChangeCompare
          v-if="businessData"
          :change-type="businessData.changeType"
          :apply-reason="businessData.applyReason"
          :submitter-name="businessData.submitterName"
          :submit-time="businessData.submitTime"
          :application-status="businessData.applicationStatus"
          :snapshot="businessData.snapshot"
          :new-data="businessData.newData"
          :field-changes="fieldChanges"
        />

        <!-- 操作区域 -->
        <a-card title="操作" class="action-card">
          <div class="action-tabs">
            <a-radio-group v-model:value="actionType" button-style="solid">
              <a-radio-button value="approve">通过</a-radio-button>
              <a-radio-button value="reject">拒绝</a-radio-button>
              <a-radio-button value="back" v-if="backableNodes.length > 0"
                >回退</a-radio-button
              >
            </a-radio-group>
          </div>

          <a-form layout="vertical">
            <!-- 回退节点选择 -->
            <a-form-item v-if="actionType === 'back'" label="回退到" required>
              <a-select
                v-model:value="form.backNodeId"
                placeholder="请选择回退节点"
                :options="backableNodes"
                :field-names="{ label: 'name', value: 'id' }"
              />
            </a-form-item>

            <!-- 操作意见 -->
            <a-form-item label="操作意见">
              <a-textarea
                v-model:value="form.comment"
                placeholder="请输入操作意见"
                :rows="3"
                :maxlength="200"
              />
            </a-form-item>
          </a-form>
        </a-card>

        <!-- 流程时间线（简要） -->
        <a-card
          title="流程记录"
          class="timeline-card"
          v-if="flowDetail?.nodeRecords?.length"
        >
          <a-timeline>
            <a-timeline-item v-for="node in flowDetail.nodeRecords" :key="node.nodeId">
              <template #dot>
                <div class="timeline-dot" :class="getDotClass(node)">
                  <component :is="getNodeIcon(node)" />
                </div>
              </template>
              <div class="timeline-content">
                <div class="node-name">{{ node.nodeName }}</div>
                <div class="operator-info">
                  {{ node.operatorName }} · {{ node.operateTime }}
                </div>
                <div v-if="node.comment" class="comment">{{ node.comment }}</div>
              </div>
            </a-timeline-item>
          </a-timeline>
        </a-card>
      </div>
    </a-spin>
  </a-modal>
</template>

<script setup>
import { ref, watch, computed, onMounted } from "vue";
import { message } from "ant-design-vue";
import {
  CheckCircleOutlined,
  CloseCircleOutlined,
  ClockCircleOutlined,
  RollbackOutlined,
} from "@ant-design/icons-vue";
import flowInstanceApi from "@/api/biz/bizFlowInstanceApi";
import deviceApi from "@/api/biz/bizDeviceApi";
import DeviceChangeCompare from "@/views/biz/device-info-management/device/components/DeviceChangeCompare.vue";
import dayjs from "dayjs";

const props = defineProps({
  visible: {
    type: Boolean,
    default: false,
  },
  taskId: {
    type: String,
    default: null,
  },
  flowInstanceId: {
    type: String,
    default: null,
  },
});

const emit = defineEmits(["update:visible", "success"]);

// 状态
const loading = ref(false);
const submitting = ref(false);
const flowDetail = ref({});
const businessData = ref(null);
const fieldChanges = ref([]);
const backableNodes = ref([]);
const actionType = ref("approve");

// 表单
const form = ref({
  comment: "",
  backNodeId: null,
});

// 字段标签映射
const fieldLabels = {
  deviceCode: "资产编号",
  deviceName: "设备名称",
  specification: "设备规格",
  deviceLevel: "设备等级",
  isKeyDevice: "是否为重点设备",
  typeId: "设备类型",
  supplierId: "供应商",
  manufacturer: "生产厂商",
  manufactureDate: "生产日期",
  factoryNo: "出厂编号",
  logisticsNo: "物流单号",
  purchaseNo: "申购单号",
  sourceType: "来源方式",
  location: "存放地点",
  deviceStatus: "设备状态",
  enableDate: "启用日期",
  factoryNodeId: "所属工厂节点",
};

// 获取变更类型颜色
const getChangeTypeColor = (type) => {
  const map = {
    新增: "green",
    编辑: "orange",
    删除: "red",
  };
  return map[type] || "default";
};

// 获取节点图标
const getNodeIcon = (node) => {
  const map = {
    4: CheckCircleOutlined,
    3: CloseCircleOutlined,
    7: RollbackOutlined,
    0: ClockCircleOutlined,
  };
  return map[node.flowCmd] || CheckCircleOutlined;
};

// 获取点样式
const getDotClass = (node) => {
  const map = {
    4: "approved",
    3: "rejected",
    7: "backed",
  };
  return map[node.flowCmd] || "";
};

// 生成字段变更对比
const generateFieldChanges = (snapshot, newData) => {
  const changes = [];

  if (!snapshot && newData) {
    // 新增：所有字段都是新增
    Object.keys(newData).forEach((key) => {
      if (
        key !== "technicalParameters" &&
        key !== "customerRequirements" &&
        key !== "maintainUserIds" &&
        key !== "maintenanceUserIds" &&
        key !== "technicalAttachmentWithCategories"
      ) {
        changes.push({
          fieldName: key,
          fieldLabel: fieldLabels[key] || key,
          oldValue: null,
          newValue: newData[key],
          changeType: "add",
        });
      }
    });
    return changes;
  }

  if (!snapshot || !newData) return changes;

  // 对比所有字段
  const allFields = new Set([...Object.keys(snapshot), ...Object.keys(newData)]);

  allFields.forEach((key) => {
    if (
      key === "technicalParameters" ||
      key === "customerRequirements" ||
      key === "maintainUserIds" ||
      key === "maintenanceUserIds" ||
      key === "technicalAttachmentWithCategories"
    )
      return;

    const oldVal = snapshot[key];
    const newVal = newData[key];

    if (oldVal === undefined && newVal !== undefined) {
      changes.push({
        fieldName: key,
        fieldLabel: fieldLabels[key] || key,
        oldValue: null,
        newValue: newVal,
        changeType: "add",
      });
    } else if (oldVal !== undefined && newVal === undefined) {
      changes.push({
        fieldName: key,
        fieldLabel: fieldLabels[key] || key,
        oldValue: oldVal,
        newValue: null,
        changeType: "delete",
      });
    } else if (JSON.stringify(oldVal) !== JSON.stringify(newVal)) {
      changes.push({
        fieldName: key,
        fieldLabel: fieldLabels[key] || key,
        oldValue: oldVal,
        newValue: newVal,
        changeType: "edit",
      });
    }
  });

  return changes;
};

// 加载流程详情
const loadFlowDetail = async () => {
  if (!props.flowInstanceId) return;

  loading.value = true;
  try {
    const res = await flowInstanceApi.getDetail({ flowInstanceId: props.flowInstanceId });
    flowDetail.value = res || {};

    // 加载业务数据
    if (flowDetail.value.businessData) {
      businessData.value = flowDetail.value.businessData;

      // 生成字段变更对比
      if (businessData.value.changeType === "编辑") {
        fieldChanges.value = generateFieldChanges(
          businessData.value.snapshot,
          businessData.value.newData
        );
      } else if (businessData.value.changeType === "新增") {
        fieldChanges.value = generateFieldChanges(null, businessData.value.newData);
      }
    }

    // 加载可回退节点
    if (flowDetail.value.flowInstance) {
      const backRes = await flowInstanceApi.getBackableNodes({
        flowInstanceId: flowDetail.value.flowInstance.id,
        currentNodeId: flowDetail.value.flowInstance.currentNodeId,
      });
      backableNodes.value = backRes || [];
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("加载流程详情失败", error);
    message.error("加载流程详情失败");
  } finally {
    loading.value = false;
  }
};

// 提交
const handleOk = async () => {
  if (actionType.value === "back" && !form.value.backNodeId) {
    message.warning("请选择回退节点");
    return;
  }

  submitting.value = true;
  try {
    const params = {
      TaskId: props.taskId,
      Comment: form.value.comment,
    };

    if (actionType.value === "approve") {
      await flowInstanceApi.approve(params);
    } else if (actionType.value === "reject") {
      await flowInstanceApi.reject(params);
    } else if (actionType.value === "back") {
      params.BackNodeId = form.value.backNodeId;
      await flowInstanceApi.back(params);
    }

    message.success("操作成功");
    emit("success");
    handleCancel();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("操作失败", error);
    message.error(error.message || "操作失败");
  } finally {
    submitting.value = false;
  }
};

// 取消
const handleCancel = () => {
  emit("update:visible", false);
  resetForm();
};

// 重置表单
const resetForm = () => {
  form.value = {
    comment: "",
    backNodeId: null,
  };
  actionType.value = "approve";
  flowDetail.value = {};
  businessData.value = null;
  fieldChanges.value = [];
};

watch(
  () => props.visible,
  (val) => {
    if (val) {
      loadFlowDetail();
    } else {
      resetForm();
    }
  }
);
</script>

<style lang="less" scoped>
.flow-process-container {
  max-height: 600px;
  overflow-y: auto;
  padding: 8px;

  .flow-info {
    margin-bottom: 16px;

    .info-item {
      .label {
        color: #999;
        margin-right: 8px;
      }
      .value {
        font-weight: 500;
      }
    }
  }

  .action-card {
    margin-bottom: 16px;

    .action-tabs {
      margin-bottom: 16px;
      text-align: center;
    }
  }

  .timeline-card {
    .timeline-dot {
      width: 24px;
      height: 24px;
      border-radius: 50%;
      display: flex;
      align-items: center;
      justify-content: center;
      background: #f0f0f0;
      color: #666;

      &.approved {
        background: #52c41a;
        color: #fff;
      }

      &.rejected {
        background: #f5222d;
        color: #fff;
      }

      &.backed {
        background: #fa8c16;
        color: #fff;
      }
    }

    .timeline-content {
      .node-name {
        font-weight: 500;
        margin-bottom: 4px;
      }

      .operator-info {
        font-size: 12px;
        color: #999;
        margin-bottom: 4px;
      }

      .comment {
        font-size: 13px;
        color: #333;
        background: #f5f5f5;
        padding: 4px 8px;
        border-radius: 4px;
      }
    }
  }
}
</style>



<template>
  <div class="device-change-compare">
    <!-- 变更概览 -->
    <a-card class="change-overview" size="small" :bordered="false">
      <a-descriptions :column="3" size="small">
        <a-descriptions-item label="变更类型">
          <a-tag :color="getChangeTypeColor(changeType)">
            {{ changeType }}
          </a-tag>
        </a-descriptions-item>
        <a-descriptions-item label="申请原因">
          {{ applyReason || "-" }}
        </a-descriptions-item>
        <a-descriptions-item label="提交时间">
          {{ formatDateTime(submitTime) }}
        </a-descriptions-item>
        <a-descriptions-item label="申请状态">
          <a-tag :color="getStatusColor(applicationStatus)">
            {{ applicationStatus }}
          </a-tag>
        </a-descriptions-item>
      </a-descriptions>
    </a-card>

    <!-- 新增模式：直接显示表单 -->
    <a-card v-if="changeType === '新增'" title="设备信息" class="device-form-card">
      <DeviceFormView :device-data="newData" />
    </a-card>

    <!-- 编辑模式：显示变更对比 -->
    <a-card v-else-if="changeType === '编辑'" title="变更内容对比" class="compare-card">
      <a-tabs v-model:activeKey="compareTab" type="card">
        <!-- 逐字段对比视图 -->
        <a-tab-pane key="field" tab="字段对比">
          <a-table
            :data-source="fieldChanges"
            :pagination="false"
            rowKey="fieldName"
            size="small"
          >
            <a-table-column title="字段名称" data-index="fieldLabel" width="150" />
            <a-table-column title="变更前" width="200">
              <template #default="{ record }">
                <div class="old-value">{{ formatFieldValue(record.oldValue) }}</div>
              </template>
            </a-table-column>
            <a-table-column title="变更后" width="200">
              <template #default="{ record }">
                <div class="new-value">{{ formatFieldValue(record.newValue) }}</div>
              </template>
            </a-table-column>
            <a-table-column title="操作类型" width="100">
              <template #default="{ record }">
                <a-tag :color="getChangeTypeColor(record.changeType)">
                  {{
                    record.changeType === "add"
                      ? "新增"
                      : record.changeType === "delete"
                      ? "删除"
                      : "修改"
                  }}
                </a-tag>
              </template>
            </a-table-column>
          </a-table>
        </a-tab-pane>

        <!-- 左右对比视图 -->
        <a-tab-pane key="side" tab="左右对比">
          <a-row :gutter="16">
            <a-col :span="12">
              <a-card title="变更前" size="small" class="compare-side">
                <DeviceFormView :device-data="snapshot" />
              </a-card>
            </a-col>
            <a-col :span="12">
              <a-card title="变更后" size="small" class="compare-side">
                <DeviceFormView :device-data="newData" />
              </a-card>
            </a-col>
          </a-row>
        </a-tab-pane>

        <!-- 技术参数对比 -->
        <a-tab-pane key="technical" tab="技术参数">
          <TechnicalParameterCompare
            :old-params="snapshot?.technicalParameters"
            :new-params="newData?.technicalParameters"
          />
        </a-tab-pane>

        <!-- 客户要求对比 -->
        <a-tab-pane key="customer" tab="客户要求">
          <CustomerRequirementCompare
            :old-reqs="snapshot?.customerRequirements"
            :new-reqs="newData?.customerRequirements"
          />
        </a-tab-pane>
      </a-tabs>
    </a-card>

    <!-- 删除模式：警告提示 -->
    <a-card v-else-if="changeType === '删除'" class="delete-warning">
      <a-alert
        message="设备删除申请"
        :description="`申请删除设备：${newData?.deviceName} (${newData?.deviceCode})`"
        type="warning"
        show-icon
      />
      <div class="delete-device-info" style="margin-top: 16px">
        <DeviceFormView :device-data="newData" />
      </div>
    </a-card>
  </div>

<script setup>
import { ref, computed } from "vue";
import DeviceFormView from "./DeviceFormView.vue";
import TechnicalParameterCompare from "@/views/biz/device-info-management/flow/components/TechnicalParameterCompare.vue";
import CustomerRequirementCompare from "@/views/biz/device-info-management/flow/components/CustomerRequirementCompare.vue";
import dayjs from "dayjs";

const props = defineProps({
  changeType: {
    type: String,
    default: "",
  },
  applyReason: {
    type: String,
    default: "",
  },
  submitterName: {
    type: String,
    default: "",
  },
  submitTime: {
    type: String,
    default: "",
  },
  applicationStatus: {
    type: String,
    default: "",
  },
  snapshot: {
    type: Object,
    default: null,
  },
  newData: {
    type: Object,
    default: null,
  },
  fieldChanges: {
    type: Array,
    default: () => [],
  },
});

const compareTab = ref("field");

// 获取变更类型颜色
const getChangeTypeColor = (type) => {
  const map = {
    新增: "green",
    编辑: "orange",
    删除: "red",
    add: "green",
    edit: "orange",
    delete: "red",
  };
  return map[type] || "default";
};

// 获取状态颜色
const getStatusColor = (status) => {
  const map = {
    草稿: "default",
    待审核: "processing",
    审核中: "processing",
    已通过: "success",
    已拒绝: "error",
    已撤销: "warning",
  };
  return map[status] || "default";
};

// 格式化日期时间
const formatDateTime = (date) => {
  return date ? dayjs(date).format("YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss") : "-";
};

// 格式化字段值
const formatFieldValue = (value) => {
  if (value === null || value === undefined) return "-";
  if (typeof value === "boolean") return value ? "是" : "否";
  if (Array.isArray(value)) return `[${value.length}项]`;
  if (typeof value === "object") {
    if (value instanceof Date) return dayjs(value).format("YYYY-MM-DD");
    return JSON.stringify(value);
  }
  return String(value);
};
</script>

      overflow-y: auto;
    }

  .old-value {
    color: #f5222d;
    text-decoration: line-through;
  }

  .new-value {
    color: #52c41a;
    font-weight: 500;
  }

  .delete-warning {
    margin-top: 16px;
  }
}
</style>

<script setup>
import { ref, reactive, onMounted, onUnmounted, computed, watch, nextTick } from "vue";
import { message, Modal } from "ant-design-vue";
import {
  SearchOutlined,
  PlusOutlined,
  RedoOutlined,
  EditOutlined,
  DeleteOutlined,
  ClockCircleOutlined,
  DownOutlined,
  CloseCircleOutlined,
  MenuOutlined,
  SettingOutlined,
  EyeOutlined,
  FilterOutlined,
} from "@ant-design/icons-vue";
import deviceApi from "@/api/biz/bizDeviceApi";
import flowInstanceApi from "@/api/biz/bizFlowInstanceApi";
import DeviceEdit from "./components/DeviceEdit.vue";
import DeviceDetail from "./components/DeviceDetail.vue";
import DeviceTypeList from "./components/DeviceTypeList.vue";
import TypeManage from "@/views/biz/device-info-management/manage/TypeManage.vue";
import { useRouter } from "vue-router";
import { debounce } from "lodash-es";
import dayjs from "dayjs";
const router = useRouter();

// 移动端检测
const isMobile = ref(false);
const searchExpanded = ref(false);
const showMobileMenu = ref(false);
const showTabBadge = ref(false);

const checkMobile = () => {
  isMobile.value = window.innerWidth <= 768;
  if (!isMobile.value) {
    searchExpanded.value = true;
    showMobileMenu.value = false;
  }
};

onMounted(() => {
  checkMobile();
  window.addEventListener("resize", checkMobile);
});

onUnmounted(() => {
  window.removeEventListener("resize", checkMobile);
});

// 当前激活的标签页
const activeTab = ref("confirmed");

// 查询参数
const searchKey = ref("");
const typeId = ref(null);
const deviceStatus = ref(null);

// 列表数据
const loading = ref(false);
const dataList = ref([]);
const pagination = reactive({
  current: 1,
  pageSize: 10,
  total: 0,
  showSizeChanger: true,
  showQuickJumper: true,
});

// 统计数量 - 只在需要时加载
const draftCount = ref(0);
const submittedCount = ref(0);
const hasLoadedDraftCount = ref(false);
const hasLoadedSubmittedCount = ref(false);

// 类型管理
const typeManageVisible = ref(false);

// 移动端分页
const mobilePagination = computed(() => ({
  current: pagination.current,
  pageSize: pagination.pageSize,
  total: pagination.total,
  onChange: (page, pageSize) => {
    pagination.current = page;
    pagination.pageSize = pageSize;
    loadData();
  },
}));

// 获取表格列
const getColumns = () => {
  const baseColumns = [
    {
      title: "设备信息",
      key: "deviceInfo",
      width: 250,
    },
    {
      title: "设备规格",
      dataIndex: "specification",
      key: "specification",
      width: 150,
    },
    {
      title: "设备类型",
      dataIndex: "typeName",
      key: "typeName",
      width: 120,
    },
    {
      title: "设备状态",
      dataIndex: "deviceStatus",
      key: "deviceStatus",
      width: 100,
    },
  ];

  // 只有我的申请标签页才显示业务状态
  if (activeTab.value === "submitted") {
    baseColumns.push({
      title: "业务状态",
      key: "businessStatus",
      width: 100,
    });
  }

  baseColumns.push({
    title: "创建时间",
    dataIndex: "creationTime",
    key: "creationTime",
    width: 160,
  });

  // 根据标签页添加不同的操作列宽度
  const actionWidths = {
    draft: 380,
    submitted: 320,
    confirmed: 280,
  };

  baseColumns.push({
    title: "操作",
    key: "action",
    width: actionWidths[activeTab.value] || 280,
    fixed: "right",
  });

  return baseColumns;
};

// 复制相关
const copyData = ref(null);

// 处理复制
const handleCopy = (record) => {
  // 保存要复制的数据
  copyData.value = record;
  // 打开新增设备抽屉，模式为 add
  editMode.value = "add";
  editVisible.value = true;
};

// 判断是否可以编辑草稿/已撤销申请
const canEditDraft = (item) => {
  // 草稿和已撤销都可以编辑
  return true;
};

// 判断是否可以删除草稿/已撤销申请
const canDeleteDraft = (item) => {
  // 草稿和已撤销都可以删除
  return true;
};

// 撤销相关
const cancelVisible = ref(false);
const cancelReason = ref("");
const canceling = ref(false);
const currentCancelItem = ref(null);

// 删除申请相关
const deleteApplyVisible = ref(false);
const deleteReason = ref("");
const deletingApply = ref(false);
const currentDeleteItem = ref(null);

// 编辑相关
const editVisible = ref(false);
const editId = ref(null);
const editMode = ref("add");

// 草稿相关
const draftEditVisible = ref(false);
const currentDraftId = ref(null);
const draftDetailVisible = ref(false);
const currentDraftDetailId = ref(null);

// 详情相关
const detailVisible = ref(false);
const detailId = ref(null);
const applyDetailVisible = ref(false);
const currentApplyId = ref(null);

// 加载列表数据（只加载当前标签页）
const loadData = async () => {
  loading.value = true;
  try {
    const params = {
      Current: pagination.current,
      Size: pagination.pageSize,
      SearchKey: searchKey.value || undefined,
      TypeId: typeId.value || undefined,
      DeviceStatus: deviceStatus.value || undefined,
    };

    let res;
    if (activeTab.value === "confirmed") {
      params.BusinessStatus = "已确认";
      res = await deviceApi.getPageList(params);

      if (res) {
        // 直接赋值，不是追加
        dataList.value = (res.records || []).map((item) => ({
          ...item,
          businessStatus: item.businessStatus,
          cancelable: false,
        }));
        pagination.total = res.total || 0;
      }
    } else if (activeTab.value === "draft") {
      // 我的草稿列表
      res = await deviceApi.getDraftList(params);

      if (res) {
        // 直接赋值，不是追加
        dataList.value = (res.records || []).map((item) => ({
          ...item,
          businessStatus: "草稿",
          applicationStatus: "草稿",
          changeType: item.changeType,
          changeApplyId: item.changeApplyId,
          deviceId: item.deviceId,
          // 确保这些字段存在
          typeName: item.typeName,
          supplierName: item.supplierName,
          factoryNodeFullPath: item.factoryNodeFullPath,
          maintainUsers: item.maintainUsers,
          maintenanceUsers: item.maintenanceUsers,
          technicalParameters: item.technicalParameters,
          customerRequirements: item.customerRequirements,
          technicalAttachmentWithCategories: item.technicalAttachmentWithCategories,
        }));
        pagination.total = res.total || 0;

        // 更新草稿数量
        draftCount.value = res.total || 0;
        hasLoadedDraftCount.value = true;
      }
    } else if (activeTab.value === "submitted") {
      // 我的申请列表
      res = await deviceApi.getSubmittedList(params);

      if (res) {
        // 直接赋值，不是追加
        dataList.value = (res.records || []).map((item) => ({
          ...item,
          businessStatus: item.applicationStatus || item.businessStatus,
          applicationStatus: item.applicationStatus,
          changeType: item.changeType,
          changeApplyId: item.changeApplyId,
          deviceId: item.deviceId,
          flowInstanceId: item.flowInstanceId,
          cancelable: item.applicationStatus === "审核中" && item.flowInstanceId,
        }));
        pagination.total = res.total || 0;

        // 更新申请数量
        submittedCount.value = res.total || 0;
        hasLoadedSubmittedCount.value = true;
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("加载设备列表失败", error);
    message.error("加载设备列表失败");
  } finally {
    loading.value = false;
  }
};

// 单独加载草稿数量（仅在需要时调用）
const loadDraftCount = async () => {
  if (hasLoadedDraftCount.value) return;
  try {
    const res = await deviceApi.getDraftList({ Current: 1, Size: 1 });
    draftCount.value = res?.total || 0;
    hasLoadedDraftCount.value = true;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("加载草稿数量失败", error);
  }
};

// 单独加载申请数量（仅在需要时调用）
const loadSubmittedCount = async () => {
  if (hasLoadedSubmittedCount.value) return;
  try {
    const res = await deviceApi.getSubmittedList({ Current: 1, Size: 1 });
    submittedCount.value = res?.total || 0;
    hasLoadedSubmittedCount.value = true;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("加载申请数量失败", error);
  }
};

// 搜索（防抖）
const handleSearch = debounce(() => {
  pagination.current = 1;
  loadData();
}, 300);

// 重置搜索
const resetSearch = () => {
  searchKey.value = "";
  deviceStatus.value = null;
  handleSearch();
};

// 类型选择
const handleTypeSelect = (selectedTypeId) => {
  typeId.value = selectedTypeId;
  if (isMobile.value) {
    showMobileMenu.value = false;
  }
  handleSearch();
};

// 打开类型管理
const openTypeManage = () => {
  typeManageVisible.value = true;
  if (isMobile.value) {
    showMobileMenu.value = false;
  }
};

// 刷新类型列表
const refreshTypeList = () => {
  typeManageVisible.value = false;
};

// 判断是否可编辑申请
const canEditApply = (item) => {
  // 删除类型不能编辑
  if (item.changeType === "删除") return false;

  // 可编辑状态：草稿、已撤销、已拒绝
  const editableStatus = ["草稿", "已撤销", "已拒绝"];
  return editableStatus.includes(item.businessStatus);
};

// 判断是否可重新申请（所有类型，状态为已撤销/已拒绝）
const canReapply = (item) => {
  const reapplyStatus = ["已撤销", "已拒绝"];
  return reapplyStatus.includes(item.businessStatus);
};

// 判断是否可删除申请记录
const canDeleteApply = (item) => {
  const deletableStatus = ["草稿", "已撤销", "已拒绝"];
  return deletableStatus.includes(item.businessStatus);
};

// 判断是否可撤销申请
const canCancelApply = (item) => {
  return item.businessStatus === "审核中";
};

// 判断详情类型
const getDetailType = (item) => {
  // 新增/编辑类型且已通过，且有设备ID，查看设备详情
  if (
    (item.changeType === "新增" || item.changeType === "编辑") &&
    item.businessStatus === "已通过" &&
    item.deviceId &&
    item.deviceId !== "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000"
  ) {
    return "device";
  }
  // 其他情况查看申请详情
  return "apply";
};

// 判断是否可查看详情
const canViewDetail = (item) => {
  // 新增/编辑类型且已通过，且有设备ID，查看设备详情
  if (
    (item.changeType === "新增" || item.changeType === "编辑") &&
    item.businessStatus === "已通过" &&
    item.deviceId
  ) {
    return true;
  }
  // 其他情况都可以查看申请详情
  return true;
};

// 判断是否可查看流程
const canViewFlow = (item) => {
  // 非草稿状态且有流程实例ID
  return item.businessStatus !== "草稿" && item.flowInstanceId;
};

// 获取操作按钮列表（移动端和桌面端统一逻辑）
const getActionButtons = (item) => {
  const buttons = [];

  // 详情按钮 - 所有申请都可以查看详情
  buttons.push({
    key: "detail",
    label: "详情",
    icon: EyeOutlined,
    handler: () => handleViewApply(item),
    show: true,
  });

  // 流程按钮 - 非草稿且有关联流程
  if (item.businessStatus !== "草稿" && item.flowInstanceId) {
    buttons.push({
      key: "flow",
      label: "流程",
      icon: ClockCircleOutlined,
      handler: () => handleViewFlow(item),
      show: true,
    });
  }

  // 可编辑状态判断
  const canEdit =
    (item.changeType === "新增" &&
      ["草稿", "已拒绝", "已撤销"].includes(item.businessStatus)) ||
    (item.changeType === "编辑" &&
      ["草稿", "已拒绝", "已撤销"].includes(item.businessStatus)) ||
    (item.changeType === "删除" &&
      ["草稿", "已拒绝", "已撤销"].includes(item.businessStatus));

  if (canEdit) {
    buttons.push({
      key: "edit",
      label: "编辑",
      icon: EditOutlined,
      handler: () => handleEditDraft(item),
      show: true,
    });
  }

  // 可撤销状态判断（审核中）
  console.log(item);
  if (item.businessStatus === "审核中") {
    buttons.push({
      key: "cancel",
      label: "撤销",
      icon: CloseCircleOutlined,
      handler: () => handleCancelApply(item),
      show: true,
    });
  }

  // 可删除状态判断 - 草稿、已撤销、已拒绝状态的申请可以直接删除申请记录
  const canDelete = ["草稿", "已撤销", "已拒绝"].includes(item.businessStatus);

  if (canDelete) {
    buttons.push({
      key: "delete",
      label: "删除",
      icon: DeleteOutlined,
      danger: true,
      handler: () => handleDeleteApplyRecord(item),
      show: true,
    });
  }

  return buttons;
};

// 处理查看详情（根据状态矩阵决定）
const handleViewItem = (item) => {
  // 新增/编辑类型且已通过 -> 查看设备详情
  if (
    (item.changeType === "新增" || item.changeType === "编辑") &&
    item.businessStatus === "已通过" &&
    item.deviceId
  ) {
    detailId.value = item.deviceId;
    detailVisible.value = true;
  }
  // 删除类型且已通过 -> 提示设备已删除
  else if (item.changeType === "删除" && item.businessStatus === "已通过") {
    message.info("该设备已被删除");
  }
  // 其他情况 -> 查看申请详情
  else {
    currentApplyId.value = item.changeApplyId;
    applyDetailVisible.value = true;
  }
};

// 处理编辑申请
const handleEditApply = (item) => {
  currentDraftId.value = item.changeApplyId;
  // 传递当前状态，如果是已拒绝，可以提示是否重置为草稿
  editMode.value = item.businessStatus === "已拒绝" ? "reject-edit" : "edit";
  draftEditVisible.value = true;
};

// 处理重新申请（删除类型的已拒绝/已撤销）
const handleReapply = (item) => {
  currentDeleteItem.value = item;
  deleteApplyVisible.value = true;
  deleteReason.value = item.applyReason || "";
};

// 处理删除申请记录
const handleDeleteApplyRecord = async (record) => {
  try {
    // 直接删除申请记录，不需要申请原因
    await deviceApi.deleteApply([record.changeApplyId]);
    message.success("删除成功");

    // 更新数量
    if (submittedCount.value > 0) {
      submittedCount.value--;
    }

    // 重新加载当前页数据
    if (dataList.value.length === 1 && pagination.current > 1) {
      pagination.current--;
    }
    loadData();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("删除失败", error);
    message.error(error.message || "删除失败");
  }
};

// 标签页切换
const handleTabChange = async () => {
  pagination.current = 1;
  // 清空数据列表
  dataList.value = [];

  // 根据切换的目标标签页加载对应的数量
  if (activeTab.value === "draft" && !hasLoadedDraftCount.value) {
    await loadDraftCount();
  } else if (activeTab.value === "submitted" && !hasLoadedSubmittedCount.value) {
    await loadSubmittedCount();
  }

  // 加载当前标签页的数据
  loadData();
};

// 表格变化
const handleTableChange = (page) => {
  pagination.current = page.current;
  pagination.pageSize = page.pageSize;
  loadData();
};

// 获取业务状态颜色
const getBusinessStatusColor = (status) => {
  const map = {
    草稿: "default",
    待审核: "processing",
    审核中: "processing",
    已确认: "success",
    已通过: "success",
    已拒绝: "error",
    已撤销: "warning",
  };
  return map[status] || "default";
};

// 新增设备档案
const handleAdd = () => {
  editMode.value = "add";
  editId.value = null;
  editVisible.value = true;
};

// 编辑设备档案
const handleEdit = (record) => {
  editMode.value = "edit";
  editId.value = record.id;
  editVisible.value = true;
};

// 编辑成功
const handleEditSuccess = () => {
  loadData();
  // 清除复制数据
  copyData.value = null;
};

// 查看设备详情
const handleView = (record) => {
  detailId.value = record.id;
  detailVisible.value = true;
};

// 草稿相关操作
const handleViewDraft = (record) => {
  currentDraftDetailId.value = record.changeApplyId;
  draftDetailVisible.value = true;
};

// 处理编辑申请（根据类型决定进入哪个界面）
const handleEditDraft = (item) => {
  // 草稿状态 -> 进入草稿编辑模式
  if (item.businessStatus === "草稿") {
    currentDraftId.value = item.changeApplyId;
    draftEditVisible.value = true;
  }
  // 已撤销/已拒绝状态 -> 根据变更类型决定进入哪个编辑界面
  else if (["已撤销", "已拒绝"].includes(item.businessStatus)) {
    if (item.changeType === "新增") {
      // 新增类型的已撤销/已拒绝 -> 进入草稿编辑模式
      currentDraftId.value = item.changeApplyId;
      draftEditVisible.value = true;
    } else if (item.changeType === "编辑") {
      // 编辑类型的已撤销/已拒绝 -> 进入设备编辑模式
      editMode.value = "edit";
      editId.value = item.id;
      editVisible.value = true;
    } else if (item.changeType === "删除") {
      // 删除类型的已撤销/已拒绝 -> 重新发起删除申请
      currentDeleteItem.value = item;
      deleteApplyVisible.value = true;
      deleteReason.value = item.applyReason || "";
    }
  }
};

// 处理删除申请记录（草稿/已撤销/已拒绝的记录）
const handleDeleteDraft = async (record) => {
  try {
    await deviceApi.deleteDraft([record.changeApplyId]);
    message.success("删除成功");

    // 更新数量
    if (activeTab.value === "draft" && draftCount.value > 0) {
      draftCount.value--;
    } else if (activeTab.value === "submitted" && submittedCount.value > 0) {
      submittedCount.value--;
    }

    // 重新加载当前页数据
    if (dataList.value.length === 1 && pagination.current > 1) {
      pagination.current--;
    }
    loadData();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("删除失败", error);
    message.error(error.message || "删除失败");
  }
};

const handleDraftSuccess = () => {
  loadData();
};

// 申请相关操作 - 查看详情
const handleViewApply = (record) => {
  // 新增/编辑类型且已通过 -> 查看设备详情
  if (
    (record.changeType === "新增" || record.changeType === "编辑") &&
    record.businessStatus === "已通过" &&
    record.deviceId &&
    record.deviceId !== "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000"
  ) {
    detailId.value = record.deviceId;
    detailVisible.value = true;
  }
  // 删除类型且已通过 -> 提示设备已删除
  else if (record.changeType === "删除" && record.businessStatus === "已通过") {
    message.info("该设备已被删除");
  }
  // 其他情况 -> 查看申请详情
  else {
    currentApplyId.value = record.changeApplyId;
    applyDetailVisible.value = true;
  }
};

// 撤销申请
const handleCancelApply = (record) => {
  if (isMobile.value) {
    currentCancelItem.value = record;
    cancelVisible.value = true;
    cancelReason.value = "";
  } else {
    Modal.confirm({
      title: "撤销申请",
      content: "确定要撤销该申请吗？",
      onOk: () => doCancelApply(record),
    });
  }
};

// 执行撤销
const doCancelApply = async (record, reason = "") => {
  try {
    await flowInstanceApi.cancel({
      flowInstanceId: record.flowInstanceId,
      reason: reason || "用户撤销",
    });
    message.success("撤销成功");

    // 更新申请数量
    if (submittedCount.value > 0) {
      submittedCount.value--;
    }

    loadData();
    return true;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("撤销失败", error);
    message.error(error.message || "撤销失败");
    return false;
  }
};

// 撤销确认
const handleCancelOk = async () => {
  canceling.value = true;
  try {
    const success = await doCancelApply(currentCancelItem.value, cancelReason.value);
    if (success) {
      cancelVisible.value = false;
    }
  } finally {
    canceling.value = false;
  }
};

// 删除申请
const handleDeleteApply = (record) => {
  if (isMobile.value) {
    currentDeleteItem.value = record;
    deleteApplyVisible.value = true;
    deleteReason.value = "";
  } else {
    Modal.confirm({
      title: "删除设备申请",
      content: "确定要发起删除该设备的申请吗？",
      onOk: () => doDeleteApply(record),
    });
  }
};

// 执行删除申请
const doDeleteApply = async (record, reason = "") => {
  try {
    await deviceApi.submitDeleteApply({
      deviceId: record.id,
      applyReason: reason || "申请删除设备",
    });
    message.success("删除申请已提交");
    loadData();
    return true;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("提交删除申请失败", error);
    message.error(error.message || "提交删除申请失败");
    return false;
  }
};

// 删除申请确认
const handleDeleteApplyOk = async () => {
  if (!deleteReason.value) {
    message.warning("请输入删除原因");
    return;
  }

  deletingApply.value = true;
  try {
    const success = await doDeleteApply(currentDeleteItem.value, deleteReason.value);
    if (success) {
      deleteApplyVisible.value = false;
    }
  } finally {
    deletingApply.value = false;
  }
};

// 查看流程
const handleViewFlow = (record) => {
  router.push(`/biz/device-info-management/flow/detail?id=${record.flowInstanceId}`);
};

// 初始化加载
onMounted(() => {
  loadData();
  // 延迟加载其他标签页的数量，不影响首屏加载
  setTimeout(() => {
    loadDraftCount();
    loadSubmittedCount();
  }, 1000);
});

// 监听搜索条件变化
watch([searchKey, typeId, deviceStatus], () => {
  handleSearch();
});
</script>

<style lang="less" scoped>
.device-management-container {
  height: 100%;
  padding: 16px;
  background: #f5f7fa;
  position: relative;

  // 移动端头部
  .mobile-header {
    position: fixed;
    top: 0;
    left: 0;
    right: 0;
    height: 50px;
    background: #fff;
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: space-between;
    padding: 0 16px;
    box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06);
    z-index: 99;

    .header-left {
      display: flex;
      align-items: center;
      gap: 12px;

      .menu-icon {
        font-size: 20px;
        color: #1890ff;
      }

      .page-title {
        font-size: 16px;
        font-weight: 500;
        color: #1f2329;
      }
    }

    .add-btn {
      border-radius: 20px;
      padding: 0 12px;
      height: 32px;
      font-size: 13px;
    }
  }

  .mobile-sidebar {
    padding: 16px 0;
  }

  .main-content {
    height: 100%;
  }

  .type-list-card {
    height: 100%;
    overflow-y: auto;
    border-radius: 12px;
