                        :value="item.id"
                      >
                        {{ item.name }}
                      </a-select-option>
                    </a-select>
                    <a-button
                      type="primary"
                      @click="openMaintainUserSelector"
                      :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                      title="选择维修人员"
                      :disabled="!isEditable"
                    >
                      <template #icon><SearchOutlined /></template>
                    </a-button>
                  </div>
                  <div
                    v-if="form.maintainUserIds && form.maintainUserIds.length > 0"
                    class="user-count-info"
                  >
                    已选择 {{ form.maintainUserIds.length }} 人
                  </div>
                </a-form-item>
              </a-col>

              <a-col :span="24" :sm="12">
                <a-form-item
                  label="保养人员"
                  name="maintenanceUserIds"
                  required
                  :validate-status="maintenanceUserError ? 'error' : ''"
                  :help="maintenanceUserError"
                >
                  <div style="display: flex; gap: 8px">
                    <a-select
                      v-model:value="form.maintenanceUserIds"
                      mode="multiple"
                      placeholder="请选择保养人员"
                      :filter-option="filterOption"
                      allow-clear
                      :max-tag-count="isMobile ? 2 : 3"
                      :disabled="!isEditable"
                      style="flex: 1"
                      @change="validateMaintenanceUsers"
                    >
                      <a-select-option
                        v-for="item in userOptions"
                        :key="item.id"
                        :value="item.id"
                      >
                        {{ item.name }}
                      </a-select-option>
                    </a-select>
                    <a-button
                      type="primary"
                      @click="openMaintenanceUserSelector"
                      :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                      title="选择保养人员"
                      :disabled="!isEditable"
                    >
                      <template #icon><SearchOutlined /></template>
                    </a-button>
                  </div>
                  <div
                    v-if="form.maintenanceUserIds && form.maintenanceUserIds.length > 0"
                    class="user-count-info"
                  >
                    已选择 {{ form.maintenanceUserIds.length }} 人
                  </div>
                </a-form-item>
              </a-col>
            </a-row>
          </a-tab-pane>
          <!-- 客户要求 -->
          <a-tab-pane key="customer" tab="客户要求">
            <div class="technical-header">
              <a-button
                type="dashed"
                @click="addCustomerRequirement"
                block
                :disabled="!isEditable"
              >
                <PlusOutlined /> 添加要求
              </a-button>
            </div>

            <div class="customer-list" v-if="form.customerRequirements?.length">
              <div
                v-for="(req, index) in form.customerRequirements"
                :key="index"
                class="customer-item"
              >
                <a-card size="small" :bordered="true">
                  <template #extra>
                    <a-button
                      type="link"
                      danger
                      size="small"
                      @click="removeCustomerRequirement(index)"
                      :disabled="!isEditable"
                    >
                      <DeleteOutlined />
                    </a-button>
                  </template>
                  <a-row :gutter="8">
                    <a-col :span="12">
                      <a-form-item
                        label="客户名称"
                        :labelCol="{ span: 24 }"
                        :wrapperCol="{ span: 24 }"
                      >
                        <a-input
                          v-model:value="req.customerName"
                          placeholder="请输入客户名称"
                          size="small"
                          :disabled="!isEditable"
                        />
                      </a-form-item>
                    </a-col>
                    <a-col :span="12">
                      <a-form-item
                        label="要求名称"
                        :labelCol="{ span: 24 }"
                        :wrapperCol="{ span: 24 }"
                      >
                        <a-input
                          v-model:value="req.requirementName"
                          placeholder="请输入要求名称"
                          size="small"
                          :disabled="!isEditable"
                        />
                      </a-form-item>
                    </a-col>
                    <a-col :span="8">
                      <a-form-item
                        label="要求值"
                        :labelCol="{ span: 24 }"
                        :wrapperCol="{ span: 24 }"
                      >
                        <a-input
                          v-model:value="req.requirementValue"
                          placeholder="要求值"
                          size="small"
                          :disabled="!isEditable"
                        />
                      </a-form-item>
                    </a-col>
                    <a-col :span="8">
                      <a-form-item
                        label="实际值"
                        :labelCol="{ span: 24 }"
                        :wrapperCol="{ span: 24 }"
                      >
                        <a-input
                          v-model:value="req.actualValue"
                          placeholder="实际值"
                          size="small"
                          :disabled="!isEditable"
                        />
                      </a-form-item>
                    </a-col>
                    <a-col :span="8">
                      <a-form-item
                        label="是否达标"
                        :labelCol="{ span: 24 }"
                        :wrapperCol="{ span: 24 }"
                      >
                        <a-checkbox
                          v-model:checked="req.isQualified"
                          :disabled="!isEditable"
                          >达标</a-checkbox
                        >
                      </a-form-item>
                    </a-col>
                  </a-row>
                </a-card>
              </div>
            </div>
            <a-empty v-else description="暂无客户要求" :image="simpleImage" />
          </a-tab-pane>

          <!-- 流程信息预览 -->
          <a-tab-pane key="flow" tab="流程预览">
            <a-alert
              message="提交后将启动以下流程"
              type="info"
              show-icon
              style="margin-bottom: 16px"
              v-if="flowNodes.length > 0"
            />

            <a-timeline v-if="flowNodes.length > 0">
              <a-timeline-item v-for="node in flowNodes" :key="node.nodeId">
                <template #dot>
                  <CheckCircleOutlined v-if="node.nodeType === 0" class="start-icon" />
                  <CheckCircleOutlined
                    v-else-if="node.nodeType === 1"
                    class="approve-icon"
                  />
                  <CopyOutlined v-else-if="node.nodeType === 2" class="copy-icon" />
                  <PlayCircleOutlined
                    v-else-if="node.nodeType === 5"
                    class="transact-icon"
                  />
                  <ForkOutlined v-else-if="node.nodeType === 9" class="end-icon" />
                </template>
                <div class="flow-node">
                  <div class="node-header">
                    <span class="node-name">{{ node.name }}</span>
                    <span class="node-type">{{ getNodeTypeName(node.nodeType) }}</span>
                  </div>

                  <!-- 审批节点详细信息 -->
                  <div
                    v-if="node.nodeType === 1 || node.nodeType === 5"
                    class="node-details"
                  >
                    <div v-if="node.approvalType === 1" class="node-badge auto-pass">
                      自动通过
                    </div>
                    <div
                      v-else-if="node.approvalType === 2"
                      class="node-badge auto-reject"
                    >
                      自动拒绝
                    </div>

                    <div v-if="node.multiInstanceApprovalType === 1" class="node-badge">
                      会签（需当前审批节点所有人同意才可通过）
                    </div>
                    <div
                      v-else-if="node.multiInstanceApprovalType === 2"
                      class="node-badge"
                    >
                      或签（一人同意即可通过该节点）
                    </div>
                    <div
                      v-else-if="node.multiInstanceApprovalType === 3"
                      class="node-badge"
                    >
                      依次审批
                    </div>

                    <div v-if="node.initiatorChoice" class="node-badge initiator-choice">
                      发起人自选
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  <!-- 审批人信息 -->
                  <div
                    v-if="node.userIds && node.userIds.length > 0"
                    class="node-assignee"
                  >
                    <span class="label">审批人：</span>
                    <span>{{ getUserNames(node.userIds) }}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div
                    v-else-if="node.roleIds && node.roleIds.length > 0"
                    class="node-assignee"
                  >
                    <span class="label">角色：</span>
                    <span>{{ node.roleIds.join("、") }}</span>
                  </div>

                  <!-- 审批人为空时的处理 -->
                  <div v-if="node.flowNodeNoAuditorType === 1" class="node-assignee">
                    <span class="label">审批人为空时：</span>
                    <span>指定人员 {{ node.flowNodeNoAuditorAssignee }}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div v-else-if="node.flowNodeNoAuditorType === 0" class="node-assignee">
                    <span class="label">审批人为空时：</span>
                    <span>自动通过</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </a-timeline-item>
            </a-timeline>

            <a-empty v-else description="暂无流程信息" :image="simpleImage" />
          </a-tab-pane>
        </a-tabs>
      </a-form>
    </a-spin>

    <template #footer>
      <div
        style="display: flex; gap: 8px; justify-content: flex-end"
        :class="{ 'mobile-footer': isMobile }"
      >
        <a-button @click="handleCancel">取消</a-button>

        <!-- 保存草稿按钮 - 只在新增模式或草稿模式显示 -->
        <a-button
          v-if="showSaveDraft && isEditable"
          @click="handleSaveDraft"
          :loading="saving"
          :disabled="saving || submitting"
        >
          保存草稿
        </a-button>

        <!-- 提交按钮 -->
        <a-button
          v-if="isEditable"
          type="primary"
          @click="handleSubmit"
          :loading="submitting"
          :disabled="submitting || saving"
        >
          {{ getSubmitButtonText }}
        </a-button>
      </div>
    </template>

    <!-- 设备类型选择器 -->
    <TypeManage
      v-model:visible="typeSelectorVisible"
      :select-mode="true"
      :selected-id="form.typeId"
      @select="handleTypeSelect"
    />

    <!-- 供应商选择器 -->
    <SupplierManage
      v-model:visible="supplierSelectorVisible"
      :select-mode="true"
      :selected-id="form.supplierId"
      @select="handleSupplierSelect"
    />

    <!-- 模板选择器 -->
    <TechnicalParameterTemplateManage
      v-model:visible="templateSelectorVisible"
      :select-mode="true"
      :selected-id="
        selectedTemplates.length > 0
          ? selectedTemplates[selectedTemplates.length - 1]
          : null
      "
      :multiple="true"
      :selected-ids="selectedTemplates"
      @select="handleTemplateSelectorSelect"
    />

    <!-- 提交确认弹窗 -->
    <a-modal
      v-model:visible="submitConfirmVisible"
      :title="isNewMode ? '提交审核' : '提交审核'"
      @ok="handleConfirmSubmit"
      @cancel="submitConfirmVisible = false"
      :confirmLoading="submitting"
      width="500px"
      :footer="null"
      :wrap-class-name="isMobile ? 'mobile-modal' : ''"
    >
      <a-form layout="vertical">
        <!-- 申请原因 - 编辑模式时需要 -->
        <a-form-item
          v-if="needApplyReason"
          label="申请原因"
          required
          :validate-status="submitReasonError ? 'error' : ''"
          :help="submitReasonError"
        >
          <a-textarea
            v-model:value="submitReason"
            placeholder="请输入申请原因"
            :rows="isMobile ? 6 : 4"
            :maxlength="200"
          />
        </a-form-item>

        <!-- 新增模式显示提示信息 -->
        <a-alert
          v-if="props.mode === 'add'"
          message="确认提交审核？"
          type="info"
          show-icon
          style="margin-bottom: 16px"
        />

        <div class="modal-footer" :class="{ 'mobile-footer': isMobile }">
          <a-button
            @click="submitConfirmVisible = false"
            :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
            >取消</a-button
          >
          <a-button
            type="primary"
            @click="handleConfirmSubmit"
            :loading="submitting"
            :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
            >确定</a-button
          >
        </div>
      </a-form>
    </a-modal>

    <!-- 添加用户选择器组件 -->
    <xn-user-selector
      ref="maintainUserSelectorRef"
      :org-tree-api="selectorApiFunction.orgTreeApi"
      :user-page-api="selectorApiFunction.userPageApi"
      :radio-model="false"
      data-type="object"
      :user-show="false"
      :multiple="true"
      @onBack="maintainUserCallBack"
    />

    <xn-user-selector
      ref="maintenanceUserSelectorRef"
      :org-tree-api="selectorApiFunction.orgTreeApi"
      :user-page-api="selectorApiFunction.userPageApi"
      :radio-model="false"
      data-type="object"
      :user-show="false"
      :multiple="true"
      @onBack="maintenanceUserCallBack"
    />
  </a-drawer>
</template>

<script setup>
import { ref, reactive, watch, computed, onMounted, onUnmounted, nextTick } from "vue";
import { message, Modal, Empty } from "ant-design-vue";
import {
  PlusOutlined,
  DeleteOutlined,
  InfoCircleOutlined,
  CheckCircleOutlined,
  PlayCircleOutlined,
  CopyOutlined,
  ForkOutlined,
  SearchOutlined,
} from "@ant-design/icons-vue";
import deviceApi from "@/api/biz/bizDeviceApi";
import typeApi from "@/api/biz/bizTypeApi";
import supplierApi from "@/api/biz/bizSupplierApi";
import factoryNodeApi from "@/api/biz/bizFactoryNodeApi";
import technicalParameterTemplateApi from "@/api/biz/bizTechnicalParameterTemplateApi";
import flowInstanceApi from "@/api/biz/bizFlowInstanceApi";
import Attachment from "@/components/Upload/index.vue";
import TypeManage from "../../manage/TypeManage.vue";
import SupplierManage from "../../manage/SupplierManage.vue";
import TechnicalParameterTemplateManage from "../../manage/TechnicalParameterTemplateManage.vue";
import tool from "@/utils/tool";
import { useOrganStore } from "@/store/organ";
import dayjs from "dayjs";
import roleApi from "@/api/sys/roleApi";
import _ from "lodash";

const { users: allUsers, getById } = useOrganStore();

// 添加用户选择器相关引用
const maintainUserSelectorRef = ref(null);
const maintenanceUserSelectorRef = ref(null);

// 人员验证错误信息
const maintainUserError = ref("");
const maintenanceUserError = ref("");

// 原始数据快照，用于比较是否有变化（仅用于编辑模式）
const originalFormData = ref(null);

// 传递选择器需要的API
const selectorApiFunction = {
  orgTreeApi: (param) => {
    return roleApi.roleOrgTreeSelector(param).then((data) => {
      return Promise.resolve(data);
    });
  },
  userPageApi: (param) => {
    return roleApi.roleUserSelector(param).then((data) => {
      return Promise.resolve(data);
    });
  },
};

// 打开维修人员选择器
const openMaintainUserSelector = () => {
  if (!isEditable.value) return;

  // 转换当前选中的用户ID为xn-user-selector需要的格式
  const selectedIds = form.maintainUserIds || [];

  // 调用xn-user-selector的显示方法
  maintainUserSelectorRef.value.showUserPlusModal(selectedIds);
};

// 打开保养人员选择器
const openMaintenanceUserSelector = () => {
  if (!isEditable.value) return;

  // 转换当前选中的用户ID为xn-user-selector需要的格式
  const selectedIds = form.maintenanceUserIds || [];

  // 调用xn-user-selector的显示方法
  maintenanceUserSelectorRef.value.showUserPlusModal(selectedIds);
};

// 维修人员选择回调
const maintainUserCallBack = (value) => {
  if (!value) {
    form.maintainUserIds = [];
    validateMaintainUsers();
    return;
  }

  // 根据value的类型进行转换
  let selectedIds = [];

  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    // 如果value是数组，可能是对象数组或ID数组
    if (value.length > 0) {
      if (typeof value[0] === "object" && value[0] !== null) {
        // 对象数组 [{id: '1', name: '张三'}, ...]
        selectedIds = value.map((item) => item.id);
      } else {
        // ID数组 ['1', '2', '3']
        selectedIds = value;
      }
    }
  } else if (typeof value === "string") {
    // 如果是逗号分隔的字符串 '1,2,3'
    selectedIds = value.split(",").filter((id) => id);
  }

  form.maintainUserIds = selectedIds;
  validateMaintainUsers();
};

// 保养人员选择回调
const maintenanceUserCallBack = (value) => {
  if (!value) {
    form.maintenanceUserIds = [];
    validateMaintenanceUsers();
    return;
  }

  // 根据value的类型进行转换
  let selectedIds = [];

  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    // 如果value是数组，可能是对象数组或ID数组
    if (value.length > 0) {
      if (typeof value[0] === "object" && value[0] !== null) {
        // 对象数组 [{id: '1', name: '张三'}, ...]
        selectedIds = value.map((item) => item.id);
      } else {
        // ID数组 ['1', '2', '3']
        selectedIds = value;
      }
    }
  } else if (typeof value === "string") {
    // 如果是逗号分隔的字符串 '1,2,3'
    selectedIds = value.split(",").filter((id) => id);
  }

  form.maintenanceUserIds = selectedIds;
  validateMaintenanceUsers();
};

// 验证维修人员
const validateMaintainUsers = () => {
  if (isEditable.value && (!form.maintainUserIds || form.maintainUserIds.length === 0)) {
    maintainUserError.value = "请选择维修人员";
    return false;
  }
  maintainUserError.value = "";
  return true;
};

// 验证保养人员
const validateMaintenanceUsers = () => {
  if (
    isEditable.value &&
    (!form.maintenanceUserIds || form.maintenanceUserIds.length === 0)
  ) {
    maintenanceUserError.value = "请选择保养人员";
    return false;
  }
  maintenanceUserError.value = "";
  return true;
};

// 根据用户ID列表获取用户名（逗号分隔）
const getUserNames = (userIds) => {
  if (!userIds || userIds.length === 0) return "";
  return userIds.map((id) => getById(id)?.name || id).join("、");
};

const props = defineProps({
  visible: {
    type: Boolean,
    default: false,
  },
  id: {
    type: String,
    default: null,
  },
  // 草稿模式：传changeApplyId
  changeApplyId: {
    type: String,
    default: null,
  },
  // 模式：add-新增设备, edit-编辑设备, draft-编辑草稿, apply-查看申请(只读)
  mode: {
    type: String,
    default: "add",
  },
  // 原申请状态
  originalStatus: {
    type: String,
    default: null,
  },
  // 复制数据（从设备档案复制时传入）
  copyData: {
    type: Object,
    default: null,
  },
});

const emit = defineEmits(["update:visible", "success"]);

// 移动端检测
const isMobile = ref(false);
const checkMobile = () => {
  isMobile.value = window.innerWidth <= 768;
};

onMounted(() => {
  checkMobile();
  window.addEventListener("resize", checkMobile);
});

onUnmounted(() => {
  window.removeEventListener("resize", checkMobile);
});

// 计算属性
const isNewMode = computed(() => {
  return props.mode === "add";
});

const isEditMode = computed(() => {
  return props.mode === "edit";
});

const isDraftMode = computed(() => {
  return props.mode === "draft";
});

const isApplyMode = computed(() => {
  return props.mode === "apply";
});

const isEditable = computed(() => {
  // 新增模式可编辑
  if (props.mode === "add") return true;
  // 编辑模式且设备状态为草稿时可编辑
  if (props.mode === "edit" && form.businessStatus === "草稿") return true;
  // 草稿模式可编辑
  if (props.mode === "draft") return true;
  // 其他情况不可编辑
  return false;
});

const getAttachmentMode = computed(() => {
  return isEditable.value ? "edit" : "view";
});

const getTitle = computed(() => {
  if (props.mode === "add") {
    // 如果有复制数据，标题显示"复制设备"
    if (props.copyData) {
      return "复制设备";
    }
    return "新增设备";
  }
  if (props.mode === "edit") {
    if (form.businessStatus === "草稿") return "编辑设备";
    return "查看设备";
  }
  if (props.mode === "draft") return "编辑草稿";
  if (props.mode === "apply") return "查看申请";
  return "设备信息";
});

// 选择器弹窗
const typeSelectorVisible = ref(false);
const supplierSelectorVisible = ref(false);
const templateSelectorVisible = ref(false);

// 打开类型选择器
const openTypeSelector = () => {
  typeSelectorVisible.value = true;
};

// 类型选择回调
const handleTypeSelect = (selected) => {
  form.typeId = selected.id;
  typeSelectorVisible.value = false;
};

// 打开供应商选择器
const openSupplierSelector = () => {
  supplierSelectorVisible.value = true;
};

// 供应商选择回调
const handleSupplierSelect = (selected) => {
  form.supplierId = selected.id;
  supplierSelectorVisible.value = false;
};

// 打开模板选择器
const openTemplateSelector = () => {
  templateSelectorVisible.value = true;
};

// 模板选择器选择回调（多选）
const handleTemplateSelectorSelect = (selected) => {
  if (Array.isArray(selected)) {
    // 多选模式
    selectedTemplates.value = selected.map((item) => item.id);
    handleTemplateChange(selectedTemplates.value);
  } else {
    // 单选模式（兼容）
    selectedTemplates.value = [selected.id];
    handleTemplateChange(selectedTemplates.value);
  }
  templateSelectorVisible.value = false;
};

// 空状态图片
const simpleImage = Empty.PRESENTED_IMAGE_SIMPLE;

// 文档分类预设
const documentCategories = [
  { label: "说明书", value: "Manual" },
  { label: "图纸", value: "Drawing" },
  { label: "技术协议", value: "TechnicalAgreement" },
  { label: "验收报告", value: "AcceptanceReport" },
  { label: "MSA报告", value: "MSAReport" },
  { label: "合格证", value: "Certificate" },
  { label: "其他", value: "Other" },
  { label: "重点设备标识表", value: "KeyEquipment" },
];

// 表单
const formRef = ref(null);
const loading = ref(false);
const saving = ref(false);
const submitting = ref(false);
const activeTab = ref("basic");
const selectedTemplates = ref([]);

// 选项数据
const typeOptions = ref([]);
const supplierOptions = ref([]);
const userOptions = ref([]);
const factoryNodeTree = ref([]);
const templateOptions = ref([]);

// 技术资料附件
const technicalAttachments = ref([]);

// 流程节点
const flowNodes = ref([]);

// 提交确认
const submitConfirmVisible = ref(false);
const submitReason = ref("");
const submitReasonError = ref("");

// 资产编号唯一性校验标记
const isDeviceCodeChecking = ref(false);
const deviceCodeUnique = ref(true);

// 表单数据
const form = reactive({
  id: null,
  deviceCode: "",
  deviceName: "",
  specification: "",
  deviceLevel: null,
  isKeyDevice: false,
  typeId: null,
  supplierId: null,
  manufacturer: "",
  manufactureDate: null,
  factoryNo: "",
  logisticsNo: "",
  purchaseNo: "",
  sourceType: "采购",
  location: "",
  deviceStatus: "未验收",
  enableDate: null,
  factoryNodeId: null,
  maintainUserIds: [],
  maintenanceUserIds: [],
  technicalParameters: [],
  customerRequirements: [],
  technicalAttachmentIds: {},
  businessStatus: "草稿",
  technicalAttachmentWithCategories: [], // 用于提交的附件数据
});

// 校验规则
const rules = computed(() => {
  // 如果是草稿模式或新增/编辑且业务状态为草稿，只校验资产编号和设备名称
  if (
    props.mode === "draft" ||
    (props.mode === "edit" && form.businessStatus === "草稿") ||
    props.mode === "add"
  ) {
    return {
      deviceCode: [
        { required: true, message: "请输入资产编号" },
        { max: 50, message: "资产编号不能超过50个字符" },
        { validator: validateDeviceCodeUnique, trigger: "blur" },
      ],
      deviceName: [
        { required: true, message: "请输入设备名称" },
        { max: 100, message: "设备名称不能超过100个字符" },
      ],
    };
  }

  // 非编辑模式（查看模式）不需要校验
  if (!isEditable.value) {
    return {};
  }

  // 提交审核时需要校验所有必填字段
  return {
    deviceCode: [
      { required: true, message: "请输入资产编号" },
      { max: 50, message: "资产编号不能超过50个字符" },
      { validator: validateDeviceCodeUnique, trigger: "blur" },
    ],
    deviceName: [
      { required: true, message: "请输入设备名称" },
      { max: 100, message: "设备名称不能超过100个字符" },
    ],
    factoryNodeId: [{ required: true, message: "请选择所属工厂位置" }],
  };
});

// 资产编号唯一性校验（增强版，检查草稿唯一性）
const validateDeviceCodeUnique = async (rule, value) => {
  if (!value || !isEditable.value) return Promise.resolve();

  // 如果是编辑自身，不需要校验唯一性
  if (props.mode === "edit" && props.id) {
    if (originalDeviceCode.value === value) {
      return Promise.resolve();
    }
  }

  if (props.mode === "draft" && props.changeApplyId) {
    // 草稿编辑，需要获取原草稿的资产编号
    if (originalDraftCode.value === value) {
      return Promise.resolve();
    }
  }

  try {
    isDeviceCodeChecking.value = true;
    const res = await deviceApi.checkDeviceCodeUnique({
      deviceCode: value,
      excludeId: props.mode === "edit" ? props.id : null,
      excludeApplyId: props.mode === "draft" ? props.changeApplyId : null,
    });

    if (!res) {
      return Promise.reject("资产编号已存在或已有相同编号的草稿");
    }
    return Promise.resolve();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("校验资产编号唯一性失败", error);
    return Promise.resolve(); // 校验失败时通过，避免阻塞
  } finally {
    isDeviceCodeChecking.value = false;
  }
};

// 检查资产编号唯一性（手动调用）
const checkDeviceCodeUnique = async () => {
  if (!form.deviceCode || !isEditable.value) return true;

  try {
    const res = await deviceApi.checkDeviceCodeUnique({
      deviceCode: form.deviceCode,
      excludeId: props.mode === "edit" ? props.id : null,
      excludeApplyId: props.mode === "draft" ? props.changeApplyId : null,
    });

    deviceCodeUnique.value = res;
    if (!res) {
      message.warning("资产编号已存在或已有相同编号的草稿");
    }
    return res;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("校验资产编号唯一性失败", error);
    return true; // 校验失败时返回 true，避免阻塞
  }
};

// 获取节点类型名称
const getNodeTypeName = (type) => {
  const map = {
    0: "开始",
    1: "审批",
    2: "抄送",
    5: "办理",
    9: "结束",
  };
  return map[type] || "未知";
};

// 加载选项数据
const loadTypeOptions = async () => {
  try {
    const res = await typeApi.getTypeList();
    typeOptions.value = res || [];
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("加载设备类型失败", error);
  }
};

const loadSupplierOptions = async () => {
  try {
    const res = await supplierApi.getSupplierList();
    supplierOptions.value = res || [];
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("加载供应商失败", error);
  }
};

const loadTemplateOptions = async () => {
  try {
    const res = await technicalParameterTemplateApi.getTechnicalParameterTemplateListForSelector();
    templateOptions.value = (res || []).map((t) => ({
      ...t,
      parameterCount: t.parameterCount || 0,
      parameters: t.parameters || [],
    }));
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("加载技术参数模板失败", error);
  }
};

const loadFactoryNodeTree = async () => {
  try {
    const res = await factoryNodeApi.getEnabledNodesForSelector();
    factoryNodeTree.value = res || [];
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("加载工厂节点树失败", error);
  }
};

const loadOptions = async () => {
  await Promise.all([
    loadTypeOptions(),
    loadSupplierOptions(),
    loadTemplateOptions(),
    loadFactoryNodeTree(),
  ]);

  // 用户列表
  const userList = tool.data.get("USER_LIST_DATA") || [];
  userOptions.value = userList;
};

// 加载流程预览
const loadFlowPreview = async () => {
  try {
    const formCode = "device";
    const params = { formCode };
    const res = await flowInstanceApi.viewProcessChart(params);
    flowNodes.value = res || [];
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("加载流程预览失败", error);
  }
};

// 转换申请详情数据为表单数据
const transformApplyData = (data) => {
  if (!data) return {};

  const newData = data.newData || {};

  return {
    id: data.deviceId,
    deviceCode: newData.deviceCode || data.deviceCode || "",
    deviceName: newData.deviceName || data.deviceName || "",
    specification: newData.specification || "",
    deviceLevel: newData.deviceLevel,
    isKeyDevice: newData.isKeyDevice || false,
    typeId: newData.typeId,
    supplierId: newData.supplierId,
    manufacturer: newData.manufacturer || "",
    manufactureDate: newData.manufactureDate ? dayjs(newData.manufactureDate) : null,
    factoryNo: newData.factoryNo || "",
    logisticsNo: newData.logisticsNo || "",
    purchaseNo: newData.purchaseNo || "",
    sourceType: newData.sourceType || "采购",
    location: newData.location || "",
    deviceStatus: newData.deviceStatus || "未验收",
    enableDate: newData.enableDate ? dayjs(newData.enableDate) : null,
    factoryNodeId: newData.factoryNodeId,
    maintainUserIds: newData.maintainUserIds || [],
    maintenanceUserIds: newData.maintenanceUserIds || [],
    technicalParameters: newData.technicalParameters || [],
    customerRequirements: newData.customerRequirements || [],
    businessStatus: data.applicationStatus || "草稿",
  };
};

// 转换草稿数据为表单数据
const transformDraftData = (data) => {
  if (!data) return {};
  const newData = data.newData || {};

  // 构建表单数据
  const formData = {
    id: data.deviceId,
    deviceCode: data.deviceCode || newData.deviceCode || "",
    deviceName: data.deviceName || newData.deviceName || "",
    specification: data.specification || newData.specification || "",
    deviceLevel: data.deviceLevel || newData.deviceLevel,
    isKeyDevice:
      data.isKeyDevice !== undefined ? data.isKeyDevice : newData.isKeyDevice || false,
    typeId: data.typeId || newData.typeId,
    supplierId: data.supplierId || newData.supplierId,
    manufacturer: data.manufacturer || newData.manufacturer || "",
    manufactureDate:
      data.manufactureDate || newData.manufactureDate
        ? dayjs(data.manufactureDate || newData.manufactureDate)
        : null,
    factoryNo: data.factoryNo || newData.factoryNo || "",
    logisticsNo: data.logisticsNo || newData.logisticsNo || "",
    purchaseNo: data.purchaseNo || newData.purchaseNo || "",
    sourceType: data.sourceType || newData.sourceType || "采购",
    location: data.location || newData.location || "",
    deviceStatus: data.deviceStatus || newData.deviceStatus || "未验收",
    enableDate:
      data.enableDate || newData.enableDate
        ? dayjs(data.enableDate || newData.enableDate)
        : null,
    factoryNodeId: data.factoryNodeId || newData.factoryNodeId,
    maintainUserIds: data.maintainUserIds || newData.maintainUserIds || [],
    maintenanceUserIds: data.maintenanceUserIds || newData.maintenanceUserIds || [],
    technicalParameters: data.technicalParameters || newData.technicalParameters || [],
    customerRequirements: data.customerRequirements || newData.customerRequirements || [],
    businessStatus: "草稿",
    technicalAttachmentWithCategories:
      data.technicalAttachmentWithCategories ||
      newData.technicalAttachmentWithCategories ||
      [],

    // 申请相关信息（用于其他判断）
    changeApplyId: data.applyId,
    changeType: data.changeType,
    applicationStatus: data.applicationStatus,
  };

  return formData;
};

// 设备信息（用于编码唯一性校验）
const deviceInfo = ref({});
const originalDeviceCode = ref("");
const originalDraftCode = ref("");

// 保存原始数据快照，用于比较是否有变化（仅用于编辑模式）
const saveOriginalData = () => {
  // 深拷贝当前表单数据作为原始快照
  originalFormData.value = _.cloneDeep({
    deviceCode: form.deviceCode,
    deviceName: form.deviceName,
    specification: form.specification,
    deviceLevel: form.deviceLevel,
    isKeyDevice: form.isKeyDevice,
    typeId: form.typeId,
    supplierId: form.supplierId,
    manufacturer: form.manufacturer,
    manufactureDate: form.manufactureDate
      ? form.manufactureDate.format("YYYY-MM-DD")
      : null,
    factoryNo: form.factoryNo,
    logisticsNo: form.logisticsNo,
    purchaseNo: form.purchaseNo,
    sourceType: form.sourceType,
    location: form.location,
    deviceStatus: form.deviceStatus,
    enableDate: form.enableDate ? form.enableDate.format("YYYY-MM-DD") : null,
    factoryNodeId: form.factoryNodeId,
    maintainUserIds: [...(form.maintainUserIds || [])],
    maintenanceUserIds: [...(form.maintenanceUserIds || [])],
    technicalParameters: _.cloneDeep(form.technicalParameters || []),
    customerRequirements: _.cloneDeep(form.customerRequirements || []),
    technicalAttachmentWithCategories: _.cloneDeep(
      form.technicalAttachmentWithCategories || []
    ),
  });
};

// 检查表单数据是否有变化（仅用于编辑模式）
const hasFormDataChanged = () => {
  if (!originalFormData.value) {
    return true;
  }

  const currentData = {
    deviceCode: form.deviceCode,
    deviceName: form.deviceName,
    specification: form.specification,
    deviceLevel: form.deviceLevel,
    isKeyDevice: form.isKeyDevice,
    typeId: form.typeId,
    supplierId: form.supplierId,
    manufacturer: form.manufacturer,
    manufactureDate: form.manufactureDate
      ? form.manufactureDate.format("YYYY-MM-DD")
      : null,
    factoryNo: form.factoryNo,
    logisticsNo: form.logisticsNo,
    purchaseNo: form.purchaseNo,
    sourceType: form.sourceType,
    location: form.location,
    deviceStatus: form.deviceStatus,
    enableDate: form.enableDate ? form.enableDate.format("YYYY-MM-DD") : null,
    factoryNodeId: form.factoryNodeId,
    maintainUserIds: [...(form.maintainUserIds || [])].sort(),
    maintenanceUserIds: [...(form.maintenanceUserIds || [])].sort(),
    technicalParameters: _.cloneDeep(form.technicalParameters || []),
    customerRequirements: _.cloneDeep(form.customerRequirements || []),
    technicalAttachmentWithCategories: _.cloneDeep(
      form.technicalAttachmentWithCategories || []
    ),
  };

  // 对原始数据进行排序，确保比较时顺序不影响结果
  const originalMaintainUserIds = [
    ...(originalFormData.value.maintainUserIds || []),
  ].sort();
  const originalMaintenanceUserIds = [
    ...(originalFormData.value.maintenanceUserIds || []),
  ].sort();

  // 分别比较各个字段
  return !(
    originalFormData.value.deviceCode === currentData.deviceCode &&
    originalFormData.value.deviceName === currentData.deviceName &&
    originalFormData.value.specification === currentData.specification &&
    originalFormData.value.deviceLevel === currentData.deviceLevel &&
    originalFormData.value.isKeyDevice === currentData.isKeyDevice &&
    originalFormData.value.typeId === currentData.typeId &&
    originalFormData.value.supplierId === currentData.supplierId &&
    originalFormData.value.manufacturer === currentData.manufacturer &&
    originalFormData.value.manufactureDate === currentData.manufactureDate &&
    originalFormData.value.factoryNo === currentData.factoryNo &&
    originalFormData.value.logisticsNo === currentData.logisticsNo &&
    originalFormData.value.purchaseNo === currentData.purchaseNo &&
    originalFormData.value.sourceType === currentData.sourceType &&
    originalFormData.value.location === currentData.location &&
    originalFormData.value.deviceStatus === currentData.deviceStatus &&
    originalFormData.value.enableDate === currentData.enableDate &&
    originalFormData.value.factoryNodeId === currentData.factoryNodeId &&
    JSON.stringify(originalMaintainUserIds) ===
      JSON.stringify(currentData.maintainUserIds) &&
    JSON.stringify(originalMaintenanceUserIds) ===
      JSON.stringify(currentData.maintenanceUserIds) &&
    _.isEqual(
      originalFormData.value.technicalParameters,
      currentData.technicalParameters
    ) &&
    _.isEqual(
      originalFormData.value.customerRequirements,
      currentData.customerRequirements
    ) &&
    _.isEqual(
      originalFormData.value.technicalAttachmentWithCategories,
      currentData.technicalAttachmentWithCategories
    )
  );
};

// 加载设备详情
const loadDetail = async () => {
  // 根据模式判断需要加载的数据
  if (props.mode === "add") {
    // 新增模式，先重置表单
    resetForm();

    // 如果有复制数据，填充表单
    if (props.copyData) {
      const copyData = props.copyData;

      // 复制其他字段（排除资产编号、设备名称和技术资料）
      form.specification = copyData.specification || "";
      form.deviceLevel = copyData.deviceLevel || null;
      form.isKeyDevice = copyData.isKeyDevice || false;
      form.typeId = copyData.typeId || null;
      form.supplierId = copyData.supplierId || null;
      form.manufacturer = copyData.manufacturer || "";
      form.manufactureDate = copyData.manufactureDate
        ? dayjs(copyData.manufactureDate)
        : null;
      form.factoryNo = copyData.factoryNo || "";
      form.logisticsNo = copyData.logisticsNo || "";
      form.purchaseNo = copyData.purchaseNo || "";
      form.sourceType = copyData.sourceType || "采购";
      form.location = copyData.location || "";
      form.deviceStatus = copyData.deviceStatus || "未验收";
      form.enableDate = copyData.enableDate ? dayjs(copyData.enableDate) : null;
      form.factoryNodeId = copyData.factoryNodeId || null;

      // 复制人员配置（只复制ID）
      // 注意：从设备详情返回的数据中，人员是在 maintainUsers 和 maintenanceUsers 数组中
      if (copyData.maintainUsers && Array.isArray(copyData.maintainUsers)) {
        form.maintainUserIds = copyData.maintainUsers.map((u) => u.userId);
      } else {
        form.maintainUserIds = copyData.maintainUserIds || [];
      }

      if (copyData.maintenanceUsers && Array.isArray(copyData.maintenanceUsers)) {
        form.maintenanceUserIds = copyData.maintenanceUsers.map((u) => u.userId);
      } else {
        form.maintenanceUserIds = copyData.maintenanceUserIds || [];
      }

      // 复制技术参数
      form.technicalParameters = copyData.technicalParameters
        ? JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(copyData.technicalParameters))
        : [];

      // 复制客户要求
      form.customerRequirements = copyData.customerRequirements
        ? JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(copyData.customerRequirements))
        : [];

      // 不复制技术资料附件
      technicalAttachments.value = [];

      // 资产编号和设备名称留空
      form.deviceCode = "";
      form.deviceName = "";

    }

    await loadFlowPreview();
    return;
  }
  if (props.mode === "edit" && !props.id) return;
  if (props.mode === "draft" && !props.changeApplyId) return;
  if (props.mode === "apply" && !props.changeApplyId && !props.id) return;

  loading.value = true;
  try {
    let res;
    if (props.mode === "edit") {
      // 设备档案编辑模式
      res = await deviceApi.getById({ id: props.id });
      deviceInfo.value = res || {};
      originalDeviceCode.value = res?.deviceCode || "";

      if (res) {
        Object.assign(form, {
          id: res.id,
          deviceCode: res.deviceCode || "",
          deviceName: res.deviceName || "",
          specification: res.specification || "",
          deviceLevel: res.deviceLevel || null,
          isKeyDevice: res.isKeyDevice || false,
          typeId: res.typeId || null,
          supplierId: res.supplierId || null,
          manufacturer: res.manufacturer || "",
          manufactureDate: res.manufactureDate ? dayjs(res.manufactureDate) : null,
          factoryNo: res.factoryNo || "",
          logisticsNo: res.logisticsNo || "",
          purchaseNo: res.purchaseNo || "",
          sourceType: res.sourceType || "采购",
          location: res.location || "",
          deviceStatus: res.deviceStatus || "未验收",
          enableDate: res.enableDate ? dayjs(res.enableDate) : null,
          factoryNodeId: res.factoryNodeId || null,
          maintainUserIds: (res.maintainUsers || []).map((u) => u.userId),
          maintenanceUserIds: (res.maintenanceUsers || []).map((u) => u.userId),
          technicalParameters: res.technicalParameters || [],
          customerRequirements: res.customerRequirements || [],
          businessStatus: res.businessStatus || "草稿",
        });

        // 加载技术资料附件
        if (res.technicalAttachments) {
          technicalAttachments.value = [];
          Object.entries(res.technicalAttachments).forEach(([category, files]) => {
            files.forEach((file) => {
              technicalAttachments.value.push({
                ...file,
                category,
              });
            });
          });
        }
      }
    } else if (props.mode === "draft") {
      // 草稿模式 - 使用 GetDraftById 接口
      res = await deviceApi.getDraftById({ applyId: props.changeApplyId });

      // 将草稿数据转换为表单格式
      const formData = transformDraftData(res);
      Object.assign(form, formData);

      // 保存原资产编号用于唯一性校验
      originalDraftCode.value = form.deviceCode;

      // 加载技术资料附件
      if (formData.technicalAttachmentWithCategories) {
        technicalAttachments.value = formData.technicalAttachmentWithCategories.map(
          (item) => ({
            attachmentId: item.attachmentId,
            id: item.attachmentId,
            fileName: item.fileName || "附件文件",
            category: item.category || "Other",
            fileSize: item.fileSize,
          })
        );
      }
    } else if (props.mode === "apply") {
      // 申请查看模式
      res = await deviceApi.getApplyDetail({
        applyId: props.changeApplyId,
        mode: "apply",
      });

      if (res && res.isSuccess && res.data) {
        const formData = transformApplyData(res.data);
        Object.assign(form, formData);

        // 加载技术资料附件
        const attachments = res.data.newData?.technicalAttachmentWithCategories || [];
        technicalAttachments.value = attachments.map((item) => ({
          attachmentId: item.attachmentId,
          id: item.attachmentId,
          fileName: item.fileName || "附件文件",
          category: item.category || "Other",
        }));
      }
    }

    // 加载流程预览
    await loadFlowPreview();

    // 对于编辑模式，保存原始数据快照
    if (props.mode === "edit") {
      await nextTick();
      saveOriginalData();
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("加载详情失败", error);
    message.error("加载详情失败");
  } finally {
    loading.value = false;
  }
};

// 模板选择变化 - 支持多选，合并参数（去重）
const handleTemplateChange = (templateIds) => {
  if (!templateIds || templateIds.length === 0 || !isEditable.value) return;

  // 收集所有选中模板的参数
  const paramMap = new Map(); // 用于去重

  templateIds.forEach((templateId) => {
    const template = templateOptions.value.find((t) => t.id === templateId);
    if (template && template.parameters) {
      template.parameters.forEach((param) => {
        // 以参数名称为key进行去重
        if (!paramMap.has(param.parameterName)) {
          paramMap.set(param.parameterName, {
            parameterName: param.parameterName,
            parameterValue: param.parameterValue || "",
          });
        }
      });
    }
  });

  // 将Map转换为数组
  const mergedParams = Array.from(paramMap.values());

  // 合并现有参数（保留已填写的值）
  const existingParams = form.technicalParameters || [];
  const mergedExistingParams = existingParams.filter(
    (p) => !paramMap.has(p.parameterName)
  );

  form.technicalParameters = [...mergedExistingParams, ...mergedParams];

  const templateNames = templateIds
    .map((id) => templateOptions.value.find((t) => t.id === id)?.templateName)
    .filter(Boolean)
    .join("、");
  message.success(
    `已应用模板 "${templateNames}" 的 ${mergedParams.length} 项参数（已去重）`
  );
};

// 添加技术参数
const addTechnicalParam = () => {
  if (!isEditable.value) return;
  if (!form.technicalParameters) {
    form.technicalParameters = [];
  }
  form.technicalParameters.push({
    parameterName: "",
    parameterValue: "",
  });
};

// 删除技术参数
const removeTechnicalParam = (index) => {
  if (!isEditable.value) return;
  form.technicalParameters.splice(index, 1);
};

// 添加客户要求
const addCustomerRequirement = () => {
  if (!isEditable.value) return;
  if (!form.customerRequirements) {
    form.customerRequirements = [];
  }
  form.customerRequirements.push({
    customerName: "",
    requirementName: "",
    requirementValue: "",
    actualValue: "",
    isQualified: false,
  });
};

// 删除客户要求
const removeCustomerRequirement = (index) => {
  if (!isEditable.value) return;
  form.customerRequirements.splice(index, 1);
};

// 附件变化
const handleAttachmentChange = () => {
  if (!isEditable.value) return;
  // 构建附件数据，用于提交
  form.technicalAttachmentWithCategories = technicalAttachments.value
    .filter((file) => file.id || file.attachmentId)
    .map((file) => ({
      attachmentId: file.id || file.attachmentId,
      category: file.category || "Other",
      fileName: file.fileName,
      fileSize: file.fileSize,
    }));
};

// 构建完整的表单数据（用于提交）
const getFormData = () => {
  return {
    deviceCode: form.deviceCode,
    deviceName: form.deviceName,
    specification: form.specification,
    deviceLevel: form.deviceLevel,
    isKeyDevice: form.isKeyDevice,
    typeId: form.typeId,
    supplierId: form.supplierId,
    manufacturer: form.manufacturer,
    manufactureDate: form.manufactureDate
      ? form.manufactureDate.format("YYYY-MM-DD")
      : null,
    factoryNo: form.factoryNo,
    logisticsNo: form.logisticsNo,
    purchaseNo: form.purchaseNo,
    sourceType: form.sourceType,
    location: form.location,
    deviceStatus: form.deviceStatus,
    enableDate: form.enableDate ? form.enableDate.format("YYYY-MM-DD") : null,
    factoryNodeId: form.factoryNodeId,
    maintainUserIds: form.maintainUserIds,
    maintenanceUserIds: form.maintenanceUserIds,
    technicalParameters: form.technicalParameters,
    customerRequirements: form.customerRequirements,
    technicalAttachmentWithCategories: form.technicalAttachmentWithCategories,
  };
};

// 过滤选项
const filterOption = (input, option) => {
  return option.children[0].toLowerCase().includes(input.toLowerCase());
};

// 跨标签页表单验证（用于提交审核）
const validateAllTabs = async () => {
  try {
    // 验证人员字段
    if (isEditable.value) {
      const isMaintainValid = validateMaintainUsers();
      const isMaintenanceValid = validateMaintenanceUsers();

      if (!isMaintainValid || !isMaintenanceValid) {
        activeTab.value = "personnel";
        throw new Error("请完善人员配置");
      }
    }
    // 验证所有必填字段
    const values = await formRef.value.validateFields();
    return { success: true, values };
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("表单验证失败", error);

    // 获取第一个验证失败的字段
    if (error.errorFields && error.errorFields.length > 0) {
      const firstError = error.errorFields[0];
      const fieldName = firstError.name[0];

      // 根据字段名切换到对应的标签页
      if (fieldName === "factoryNodeId") {
        activeTab.value = "basic";
      } else if (["deviceCode", "deviceName"].includes(fieldName)) {
        activeTab.value = "basic";
      }

      // 显示错误提示
      message.error(firstError.errors[0]);
    }

    throw error;
  }
};

// 保存草稿 - 只在校验资产编号和设备名称
const handleSaveDraft = async () => {
  if (!isEditable.value) return;

  try {
    // 再次校验设备编号唯一性
    const isUnique = await checkDeviceCodeUnique();
    if (!isUnique) {
      message.error("资产编号已存在或已有相同编号的草稿");
      return;
    }

    // 草稿保存只验证资产编号和设备名称
    await formRef.value.validateFields(["deviceCode", "deviceName"]);

    saving.value = true;
    const formData = getFormData();

    if (props.mode === "draft" && props.changeApplyId) {
      // 更新草稿
      await deviceApi.updateDraft({
        changeApplyId: props.changeApplyId,
        formData: formData,
      });
    } else {
      // 新增草稿
      await deviceApi.saveDraft(formData);
    }

    message.success("草稿保存成功");
    emit("success");
    handleCancel();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("保存草稿失败", error);
    if (error.errorFields) {
      message.error("请填写资产编号和设备名称");
    } else {
      message.error(error.message || "保存草稿失败");
    }
  } finally {
    saving.value = false;
  }
};

// 修改计算属性，根据模式决定是否显示保存草稿按钮
const showSaveDraft = computed(() => {
  // 新增模式 - 可以保存草稿
  if (props.mode === "add") {
    return true;
  }

  // 草稿模式 - 可以保存草稿
  if (props.mode === "draft") {
    return true;
  }

  // 编辑设备档案 - 不显示保存草稿按钮
  if (props.mode === "edit") {
    return false;
  }

  // 申请查看模式 - 不显示保存草稿按钮
  if (props.mode === "apply") {
    return false;
  }

  return false;
});

// 获取提交按钮文本
const getSubmitButtonText = computed(() => {
  if (props.mode === "add") return "提交审核";
  if (props.mode === "edit") return "提交审核";
  if (props.mode === "draft") return "提交审核";
  return "提交";
});

// 判断是否需要申请原因
const needApplyReason = computed(() => {
  // 编辑设备档案时需要申请原因
  if (props.mode === "edit") return true;
  // 草稿模式且已有设备ID（编辑已有设备的草稿）时需要申请原因
  if (props.mode === "draft" && form.id) return true;
  return false;
});

// 提交审核
const handleSubmit = async () => {
  if (!isEditable.value) return;

  try {
    // 再次校验设备编号唯一性
    const isUnique = await checkDeviceCodeUnique();
    if (!isUnique) {
      message.error("资产编号已存在或已有相同编号的草稿");
      return;
    }

    // 对于编辑模式，检查数据是否有变化
    if (props.mode === "edit") {
      if (!hasFormDataChanged()) {
        message.warning("数据没有发生变化，无需提交审核");
        return;
      }
    }

    // 验证所有必填字段
    await validateAllTabs();

    submitConfirmVisible.value = true;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("表单验证失败", error);
  }
};

// 确认提交
const handleConfirmSubmit = async () => {
  // 需要申请原因时检查
  if (needApplyReason.value && !submitReason.value) {
    submitReasonError.value = "请输入申请原因";
    return;
  }

  submitting.value = true;
  try {
    const formData = getFormData();

    // 构建提交数据
    const submitData = {
      changeType: props.mode === "add" ? "新增" : "编辑",
      applyReason: submitReason.value,
      formData: formData,
    };

    // 如果是编辑已有设备，传入设备ID
    if (props.mode === "edit" && props.id) {
      submitData.deviceId = props.id;
    }

    // 如果是草稿模式，传入草稿ID
    if (props.mode === "draft" && props.changeApplyId) {
      submitData.changeApplyId = props.changeApplyId;
    }

    // 如果是从设备档案编辑且设备已有ID，传入设备ID
    if (form.id) {
      submitData.deviceId = form.id;
    }

    await deviceApi.submitApply(submitData);

    message.success("提交成功");
    submitConfirmVisible.value = false;
    emit("success");
    handleCancel();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("提交失败", error);
    message.error(error.message || "提交失败");
  } finally {
    submitting.value = false;
  }
};

// 取消
const handleCancel = () => {
  emit("update:visible", false);
};

// 重置表单
const resetForm = () => {
  form.id = null;
  form.deviceCode = "";
  form.deviceName = "";
  form.specification = "";
  form.deviceLevel = null;
  form.isKeyDevice = false;
  form.typeId = null;
  form.supplierId = null;
  form.manufacturer = "";
  form.manufactureDate = null;
  form.factoryNo = "";
  form.logisticsNo = "";
  form.purchaseNo = "";
  form.sourceType = "采购";
  form.location = "";
  form.deviceStatus = "未验收";
  form.enableDate = null;
  form.factoryNodeId = null;
  form.maintainUserIds = [];
  form.maintenanceUserIds = [];
  form.technicalParameters = [];
  form.customerRequirements = [];
  form.technicalAttachmentIds = {};
  form.businessStatus = "草稿";
  form.technicalAttachmentWithCategories = [];

  technicalAttachments.value = [];
  selectedTemplates.value = [];
  flowNodes.value = [];
  activeTab.value = "basic";
  submitReason.value = "";
  submitReasonError.value = "";
  deviceCodeUnique.value = true;
  originalDeviceCode.value = "";
  originalDraftCode.value = "";
  originalFormData.value = null;
};

// 监听设备编号变化，重置错误状态
watch(
  () => form.deviceCode,
  () => {
    if (deviceCodeUnique.value === false) {
      deviceCodeUnique.value = true;
    }
  }
);

// 监听 form.maintainUserIds 变化
watch(
  () => form.maintainUserIds,
  (newVal) => {
    if (newVal && newVal.length > 0) {
      maintainUserError.value = "";
    }
  }
);

// 监听 form.maintenanceUserIds 变化
watch(
  () => form.maintenanceUserIds,
  (newVal) => {
    if (newVal && newVal.length > 0) {
      maintenanceUserError.value = "";
    }
  }
);

// 监听自定义提交事件
const handleTriggerSubmit = (event) => {
  if (event.detail.id === props.id) {
    handleSubmit();
  }
};

onMounted(() => {
  window.addEventListener("trigger-submit", handleTriggerSubmit);
});

onUnmounted(() => {
  window.removeEventListener("trigger-submit", handleTriggerSubmit);
});

watch(
  () => props.visible,
  (val) => {
    if (val) {
      loadOptions();
      checkMobile();
      loadDetail();
    } else {
      // 关闭时重置表单
      resetForm();
    }
  }
);

watch(
  technicalAttachments,
  (newVal) => {
    handleAttachmentChange();
  },
  { deep: true, immediate: true }
);

watch(submitReason, () => {
  if (submitReasonError.value) {
    submitReasonError.value = "";
  }
});
</script>

<template>

    :open="visible"

                  <div class="label">创建人</div>

              </div>
            </a-collapse-panel>

            <!-- 技术参数 -->
            <a-collapse-panel
